+1,370 @@\n+//! Lint command for beads_zig.\n+//!\n+//! `bz lint` - Validate database consistency\n+//!\n+//! Performs comprehensive validation checks on the issue database:\n+//! - ID format validation\n+//! - Orphaned hierarchical children\n+//! - Orphaned dependencies\n+//! - Circular dependencies\n+//! - Empty or invalid titles\n+//! - Duplicate content hashes\n+//! - Invalid status combinations\n+//! - Future timestamps\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const storage = @import(\"../storage/mod.zig\");\n+const common = @import(\"common.zig\");\n+const args = @import(\"args.zig\");\n+const id_mod = @import(\"../id/mod.zig\");\n+const orphans = @import(\"orphans.zig\");\n+\n+const IssueStore = common.IssueStore;\n+const DependencyGraph = storage.DependencyGraph;\n+const CommandContext = common.CommandContext;\n+\n+pub const LintError = error{\n+    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n+    StorageError,\n+    OutOfMemory,\n+};\n+\n+pub const LintIssue = struct {\n+    id: ?[]const u8,\n+    severity: []const u8, // \"error\", \"warning\", \"info\"\n+    category: []const u8,\n+    message: []const u8,\n+};\n+\n+pub const LintResult = struct {\n+    success: bool,\n+    issues: ?[]const LintIssue = null,\n+    errors: usize = 0,\n+    warnings: usize = 0,\n+    infos: usize = 0,\n+    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n+};\n+\n+pub fn run(\n+    cmd_args: args.LintArgs,\n+    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+) !void {\n+    var ctx = (try CommandContext.init(allocator, global)) orelse {\n+        return LintError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n+    };\n+    defer ctx.deinit();\n+\n+    var issues: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue) = .{};\n+    defer issues.deinit(allocator);\n+\n+    // Run all lint checks\n+    try lintIdFormats(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n+    try lintOrphanedHierarchy(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n+    try lintOrphanedDependencies(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n+    try lintCircularDependencies(&ctx, allocator, &issues);\n+    try lintTitles(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n+    try lintDuplicateHashes(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n+    try lintStatusConsistency(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n+    try lintTimestamps(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n+\n+    // Count by severity\n+    var errors: usize = 0;\n+    var warnings: usize = 0;\n+    var infos: usize = 0;\n+\n+    for (issues.items) |issue| {\n+        if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"error\")) {\n+            errors += 1;\n+        } else if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"warning\")) {\n+            warnings += 1;\n+        } else {\n+            infos += 1;\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    // Apply limit if specified\n+    const display_issues = if (cmd_args.limit) |limit|\n+        issues.items[0..@min(limit, issues.items.len)]\n+    else\n+        issues.items;\n+\n+    if (global.isStructuredOutput()) {\n+        try ctx.output.printJson(LintResult{\n+            .success = errors == 0,\n+            .issues = display_issues,\n+            .errors = errors,\n+            .warnings = warnings,\n+            .infos = infos,\n+        });\n+    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n+        if (issues.items.len == 0) {\n+            try ctx.output.println(\"No issues found. Database is consistent.\", .{});\n+        } else {\n+            try ctx.output.println(\"Database Lint Results\", .{});\n+            try ctx.output.print(\"\\n\", .{});\n+\n+            for (display_issues) |issue| {\n+                const icon = if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"error\"))\n+                    \"[ERR] \"\n+                else if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"warning\"))\n+                    \"[WARN]\"\n+                else\n+                    \"[INFO]\";\n+\n+                if (issue.id) |id| {\n+                    try ctx.output.print(\"{s} {s}: {s}\\n\", .{ icon, id, issue.message });\n+                } else {\n+                    try ctx.output.print(\"{s} {s}\\n\", .{ icon, issue.message });\n+                }\n+            }\n+\n+            try ctx.output.print(\"\\nSummary: {d} error(s), {d} warning(s), {d} info(s)\\n\", .{ errors, warnings, infos });\n+\n+            if (cmd_args.limit) |limit| {\n+                if (issues.items.len > limit) {\n+                    try ctx.output.print(\"(showing {d} of {d}, use --limit to see more)\\n\", .{ limit, issues.items.len });\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+fn lintIdFormats(\n+    store: *IssueStore,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n+) !void {\n+    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n+        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n+\n+        if (!id_mod.validateId(issue.id)) {\n+            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n+                .id = issue.id,\n+                .severity = \"error\",\n+                .category = \"id_format\",\n+                .message = \"Invalid issue ID format\",\n+            });\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+fn lintOrphanedHierarchy(\n+    store: *IssueStore,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n+) !void {\n+    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n+        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n+\n+        if (orphans.getParentId(issue.id)) |parent_id| {\n+            if (!store.id_index.contains(parent_id)) {\n+                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n+                    .id = issue.id,\n+                    .severity = \"warning\",\n+                    .category = \"orphan_hierarchy\",\n+                    .message = \"Parent issue does not exist\",\n+                });\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+fn lintOrphanedDependencies(\n+    store: *IssueStore,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n+) !void {\n+    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n+        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n+\n+        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n+            if (!store.id_index.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n+                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n+                    .id = issue.id,\n+                    .severity = \"warning\",\n+                    .category = \"orphan_dependency\",\n+                    .message = \"Dependency references non-existent issue\",\n+                });\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+fn lintCircularDependencies(\n+    ctx: *CommandContext,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n+) !void {\n+    var graph = ctx.createGraph();\n+    const cycles = try graph.detectCycles();\n+    defer if (cycles) |c| allocator.free(c);\n+\n+    if (cycles) |cycle_list| {\n+        if (cycle_list.len > 0) {\n+            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n+                .id = null,\n+                .severity = \"error\",\n+                .category = \"circular_dependency\",\n+                .message = \"Circular dependencies detected in dependency graph\",\n+            });\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+fn lintTitles(\n+    store: *IssueStore,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n+) !void {\n+    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n+        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n+\n+        if (issue.title.len == 0) {\n+            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n+                .id = issue.id,\n+                .severity = \"error\",\n+                .category = \"empty_title\",\n+                .message = \"Issue has empty title\",\n+            });\n+        } else if (issue.title.len > 500) {\n+            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n+                .id = issue.id,\n+                .severity = \"warning\",\n+                .category = \"long_title\",\n+                .message = \"Title exceeds 500 character limit\",\n+            });\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+fn lintDuplicateHashes(\n+    store: *IssueStore,\n+    allocator: Orphans command for beads_zig.\n+//!\n+//! `bz orphans` - Find issues with missing parent references\n+//!\n+//! Detects orphaned issues in two ways:\n+//! 1. Hierarchical orphans: Child issues (e.g., bd-abc.1) whose parent (bd-abc) doesn't exist\n+//! 2. Dependency orphans: Issues referencing non-existent depends_on_id targets\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const common = @import(\"common.zig\");\n+const args = @import(\"args.zig\");\n+\n+const {\n+            try ctx.output.println(\"No orphaned issues found.\", .{});\n+        } else {\n+            try ctx.output.println(\"Found {d} orphaned issue(s):\", .{orphans.items.len});\n+ .issues = display_issues,\n+            .errors = errors,\n+            .warnings = warnings,\n+            .infos = infos,\n+        });\n+    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n+        if 60);\n+\n+    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n+        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n+\n+        // Check for timestamps too far in the future (more than 1 day)\n+        if Orphans command for beads_zig.\n+//!\n+//! `bz orphans` - Find issues with missing parent references\n+//!\n+//! Detects orphaned issues in two ways:\n+//! 1. Hierarchical orphans: Child issues (e.g., bd-abc.1) whose parent (bd-abc) doesn't exist\n+//! 2. Dependency orphans: Issues referencing non-existent depends_on_id targets\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const common = @import(\"common.zig\");\n+const args = @import(\"args.zig\");\n+\n+const IssueStore = common.IssueStore;\n+const CommandContext = common.CommandContext;\n+\n+pub const OrphansError = error{\n+    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n+    StorageError,\n+    OutOfMemory,\n+};\n+\n+pub const OrphanInfo = struct {\n+    id: []const u8,\n+    orphan_type: []const u8,\n+    missing_ref: []const u8,\n+    title: []const u8,\n+};\n+\n+pub const OrphansResult = struct {\n+    success: bool,\n+    orphans: ?[]const OrphanInfo = null,\n+    count: usize = 0,\n+    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n+};\n+\n+pub fn run(\n+    cmd_args: args.OrphansArgs,\n+    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+) !void {\n+    var ctx = (try CommandContext.init(allocator, global)) orelse {\n+        return OrphansError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n+    };\n+    defer ctx.deinit();\n+\n+    var orphans: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(OrphanInfo) = .{};\n+    defer orphans.deinit(allocator);\n+\n+    // Check for hierarchical orphans (child IDs with missing parents)\n+    if (!cmd_args.deps_only) {\n+        try findHierarchicalOrphans(&ctx.store, allocator, &orphans);\n+    }\n+\n+    // Check for dependency orphans (dependencies pointing to non-existent issues)\n+    if (!cmd_args.hierarchy_only) {\n+        try findDependencyOrphans(&ctx.store, allocator, &orphans);\n+    }\n+\n+    // Apply limit if specified\n+    const display_orphans = if (cmd_args.limit) |limit|\n+        orphans.items[0..@min(limit, orphans.items.len)]\n+    else\n+        orphans.items;\n+\n+    if (global.isStructuredOutput()) {\n+        try ctx.output.printJson(OrphansResult{\n+            .success = true,\n+            .orphans = display_orphans,\n+            .count = orphans.items.len,\n+        });\n+    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n+        if (orphans.items.len == 0) {\n+            try ctx.output.println(\"No orphaned issues found.\", .{});\n+        } else {\n+            try ctx.output.println(\"Found {d} orphaned issue(s):\", .{orphans.items.len});\n+            try ctx.output.print(\"\\n\", .{});\n+\n+            for (display_orphans) |orphan| {\n+                try ctx.output.print(\"{s}  [{s}]\\n\", .{ orphan.id, orphan.orphan_type });\n+ .{});\n+            }\n+\n+            if (cmd_args.limit) |limit| {\n+                if (orphans.items.len > limit) {\n+                    try ctx.output.print(\"(showing {d} of {d}, use --limit to see more)\\n\", .{ limit, orphans.items.len });\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+/// Find issues with hierarchical IDs whose parent doesn't exist.\n+/// Example: bd-abc.1 exists but bd-abc doesn't.\n+fn findHierarchicalOrphans(\n+    store: *IssueStore,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+    orphans: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(OrphanInfo),\n+) !void {\n+ |parent_id| {\n+            // Parent ID found - check if parent exists\n+            if (!store.id_index.contains(parent_id)) {\n+                try orphans.append(allocator, .{\n+                    .id = issue.id,\n+                    .orphan_type = \"hierarchy\",\n+                    .missing_ref = parent_id,\n+                    .title = issue.title,\n+                });\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+/// Find issues with dependencies pointing to non-existent issues.\n+fn findDependencyOrphans(\n+    store: *IssueStore,\n+    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n+    orphans: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(OrphanInfo),\n+) !void {\n+    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n+        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n+\n+        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n+            if (!store.id_index.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n+                try orphans.append(allocator, .{\n+                    .id = issue.id,\n+                    .orphan_type = \"dependency\",\n+                    .missing_ref = dep.depends_on_id,\n+                    .title = issue.title,\n+                });\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+/// Extract the parent ID from a hierarchical child ID.\n+/// Returns null if this is a top-level ID (no parent).\n+/// Example: \"bd-abc.1\" -> \"bd-abc\", \"bd-abc.1.2\" -> \"bd-abc.1\"\n+pub fn getParentId(id: Hierarchical orphans: Child issues (e.g., bd-abc.1) whose parent (bd-abc) doesn't exist\n//! 2. Dependency orphans: Issues referencing non-existent depends_on_id targets\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst common = @import(\"common.zig\");\nconst args = @import(\"args.zig\");\n\nconst IssueStore = common.IssueStore;\nconst CommandContext = common.CommandContext;\n\npub const OrphansError = error{\n    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n    StorageError,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\npub const OrphanInfo = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n    orphan_type: []const u8,\n    missing_ref: []const u8,\n    title: []const u8,\n};\n\npub const OrphansResult = struct {\n    success: bool,\n std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var ctx = (try CommandContext.init(allocator, global)) orelse {\n        return OrphansError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n    };\n    defer ctx.deinit();\n\n    var orphans: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(OrphanInfo) = .{};\n    defer orphans.deinit(allocator);\n\n    // Check for hierarchical orphans (child IDs with missing parents)\n    if (!cmd_args.deps_only) {\n        try findHierarchicalOrphans(&ctx.store, allocator, &orphans);\n    }\n\n    // Check for dependency orphans (dependencies pointing to non-existent issues)\n    if (!cmd_args.hierarchy_only) {\n        try findDependencyOrphans(&ctx.store, allocator, &orphans);\n    }\n\n    // Apply limit if specified\n    const display_orphans = if (cmd_args.limit) |limit|\n        orphans.items[0..@min(limit, });\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Find issues with hierarchical IDs whose parent doesn't exist.\n/// Example: bd-abc.1 exists but bd-abc doesn't.\nfn findHierarchicalOrphans(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    orphans: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(OrphanInfo),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        // Check if this is a child issue (has a dot in the ID)\n        if (getParentId(issue.id)) |parent_id| {\n            // Parent ID found - check if std.mem.lastIndexOf(u8, id, \".\");\n    if (last_dot) |dot_pos| {\n        // Verify there's something before the dot\n        if (dot_pos > 0) {\n            return id[0..dot_pos];\n        }\n (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n            if (!store.id_index.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"warning\",\n                    .category = \"orphan_dependency\",\n                    .message = \"Dependency references non-existent issue\",\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintCircularDependencies(\n    ctx: *CommandContext,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    var graph = ctx.createGraph();\n    const cycles = try graph.detectCycles();\n    defer if (cycles) |c| allocator.free(c);\n\n    if (cycles) |cycle_list| {\n        if (cycle_list.len > 0) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = null,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"circular_dependency\",\n                .message = \"Circular dependencies detected in dependency graph\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintTitles(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (issue.title.len == 0) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"empty_title\",\n                .message = \"Issue has empty title\",\n            });\n        } else if (issue.title.len > 500) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"long_title\",\n                .message = \"Title exceeds 500 character limit\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintDuplicateHashes(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    var hash_map = std.StringHashMap([]const u8).init(allocator);\n    defer hash_map.deinit();\n\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (issue.content_hash) |hash| {\n            if (hash_map.get(hash)) |existing_id| {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"info\",\n                    .category = \"duplicate_hash\",\n                    .message = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"Duplicate content hash with {s}\", .{existing_id}),\n                });\n            } else {\n                try hash_map.put(hash, issue.id);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintStatusConsistency(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        // Closed issues should have closed_at timestamp\n        if (issue.status.eql(.closed) and issue.closed_at.value == null) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"status_consistency\",\n                .message = \"Closed issue missing closed_at timestamp\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Deferred issues should have defer_until\n        if (issue.status.eql(.deferred) and issue.defer_until.value == null) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"info\",\n                .category = \"status_consistency\",\n                .message = \"Deferred issue missing defer_until date\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintTimestamps(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    const one_day_future = now + (24 * 60 * 60);\n\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        // Check for timestamps too far in the future (more than 1 day)\n        if (issue.created_at.value > one_day_future) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"future_timestamp\",\n                .message = \"created_at timestamp is in the future\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        if (issue.updated_at.value > one_day_future) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"future_timestamp\",\n                .message = \"updated_at timestamp is in the future\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Check that updated_at >= created_at\n        if (issue.updated_at.value < issue.created_at.value) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"timestamp_order\",\n                .message = \"updated_at is before created_at\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"LintResult struct works\" {\n    const result = LintResult{\n        .success = true,\n        .errors = 0,\n        .warnings = 0,\n        .infos = 0,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(result.success);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), result.errors);\n}\n\ntest \"LintIssue struct works\" {\n    const issue = LintIssue{\n        .id = \"bd-abc\",\n        .severity = \"error\",\n        .category = \"id_format\",\n        .message = \"Invalid ID\",\n    };\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc\", issue.id.?);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"error\", issue.severity);\n}\n\ntest \"run detects uninitialized workspace\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const cmd_args = args.LintArgs{};\n    const global = args.GlobalOptions{ .silent = true, .data_path = \"/nonexistent/path\" };\n\n    const result = run(cmd_args, global, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expectError(LintError.WorkspaceNotInitialized, result);\n}\n","numLines":371,"startLine":1,"totalLines":371}}}

  var infos: usize = 0;\n\n    for (issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"error\")) {\n            errors += 1;\n        } else if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, Database is consistent.\", .{});\n        } else {\n            try ctx.output.println(\"Database Lint Results\", .{});\n            try ctx.output.print(\"\\n\", .{});\n\n            for limit) {\n                    try ctx.output.print(\"(showing {d} of {d}, use --limit to see more)\\n\", .{ limit, issues.items.len });\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintIdFormats(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (!id_mod.validateId(issue.id)) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"id_format\",\n                .message = \"Invalid issue ID format\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintOrphanedHierarchy(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (orphans.getParentId(issue.id)) |parent_id| {\n            if (!store.id_index.contains(parent_id)) {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"warning\",\n                    .category = \"orphan_hierarchy\",\n                    .message = \"Parent issue does not exist\",\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintOrphanedDependencies(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n            if (!store.id_index.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"warning\",\n                    .category = \"orphan_dependency\",\n                    .message = \"Dependency references non-existent issue\",\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintCircularDependencies(\n    ctx: *CommandContext,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    var graph = ctx.createGraph();\n    const cycles = try graph.detectCycles();\n    defer if (cycles) |c| allocator.free(c);\n\n    if (cycles) |cycle_list| {\n        if (cycle_list.len > 0) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = null,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"circular_dependency\",\n                .message = \"Circular dependencies detected in dependency graph\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintTitles(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (issue.title.len == 0) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"empty_title\",\n                .message = \"Issue has empty title\",\n            });\n        } else if (issue.title.len > 500) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"long_title\",\n                .message = \"Title exceeds 500 character limit\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintDuplicateHashes(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    var hash_map = std.StringHashMap([]const u8).init(allocator);\n    defer hash_map.deinit();\n\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (issue.content_hash) |hash| {\n            if (hash_map.get(hash)) |existing_id| {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"info\",\n                    .category = \"duplicate_hash\",\n                    .message = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"Duplicate content hash with {s}\", .{existing_id}),\n                });\n            } else {\n                try hash_map.put(hash, issue.id);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintStatusConsistency(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        // Closed issues should have closed_at timestamp\n        if (issue.status.eql(.closed) and issue.closed_at.value == null) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"status_consistency\",\n                .message = \"Closed issue missing closed_at timestamp\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Deferred issues should have defer_until\n        if (issue.status.eql(.deferred) and issue.defer_until.value == null) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"info\",\n                .category = \"status_consistency\",\n                .message = \"Deferred issue missing defer_until date\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintTimestamps(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    const one_day_future = now + (24 * 60 * 60);\n\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        // Check for timestamps too far in the future (more than 1 day)\n        if (issue.created_at.value > one_day_future) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"future_timestamp\",\n                .message = \"created_at timestamp is in the future\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        if (issue.updated_at.value > one_day_future) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"future_timestamp\",\n                .message = \"updated_at timestamp is in the future\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Check that updated_at >= created_at\n        if (issue.updated_at.value < issue.created_at.value) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"timestamp_order\",\n                .message = \"updated_at is before created_at\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"LintResult struct works\" {\n    const result = LintResult{\n        .success = true,\n        .errors = 0,\n        .warnings = 0,\n        .infos = 0,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(result.success);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), result.errors);\n}\n\ntest \"LintIssue struct works\" {\n    const issue = LintIssue{\n        .id = \"bd-abc\",\n        .severity = \"error\",\n        .category = \"id_format\",\n        .message = \"Invalid ID\",\n    };\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc\", issue.id.?);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"error\", issue.severity);\n}\n\ntest \"run detects uninitialized workspace\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const cmd_args = args.LintArgs{};\n    const global = args.GlobalOptions{    issues: ?[]const LintIssue = null,\n    errors: usize = 0,\n    warnings: usize = 0,\n    infos: usize = 0,\n    message: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\npub fn run(\n    cmd_args: args.LintArgs,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    var ctx = (try CommandContext.init(allocator, global)) orelse {\n        return LintError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n    };\n    defer ctx.deinit();\n\n    var issues: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue) = .{};\n    defer issues.deinit(allocator);\n\n    // Run all lint checks\n    try lintIdFormats(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n    try lintOrphanedHierarchy(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n    try lintOrphanedDependencies(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n    try lintCircularDependencies(&ctx, allocator, &issues);\n    try lintTitles(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n    try lintDuplicateHashes(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n    try lintStatusConsistency(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n    try lintTimestamps(&ctx.store, allocator, &issues);\n\n    // Count by severity\n    var errors: usize = 0;\n    var warnings: usize = 0;\n    var infos: usize = 0;\n\n    for (issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"error\")) {\n            errors += 1;\n        } else if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"warning\")) {\n            warnings += 1;\n        } else {\n            infos += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Apply limit if specified\n    const display_issues = if (cmd_args.limit) |limit|\n        issues.items[0..@min(limit, issues.items.len)]\n    else\n        issues.items;\n\n    if (global.isStructuredOutput()) {\n        try ctx.output.printJson(LintResult{\n            .success = errors == 0,\n            .issues = display_issues,\n            .errors = errors,\n            .warnings = warnings,\n            .infos = infos,\n        });\n    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n        if (issues.items.len == 0) {\n            try ctx.output.println(\"No issues found. Database is consistent.\", .{});\n        } else {\n            try ctx.output.println(\"Database Lint Results\", .{});\n            try ctx.output.print(\"\\n\", .{});\n\n            for (display_issues) |issue| {\n                const icon = if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"error\"))\n                    \"[ERR] \"\n                else if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.severity, \"warning\"))\n                    \"[WARN]\"\n                else\n                    \"[INFO]\";\n\n                if (issue.id) |id| {\n                    try ctx.output.print(\"{s} {s}: {s}\\n\", .{ icon, id, issue.message });\n                } else {\n                    try ctx.output.print(\"{s} {s}\\n\", .{ icon, issue.message });\n                }\n            }\n\n            try ctx.output.print(\"\\nSummary: {d} error(s), {d} warning(s), {d} info(s)\\n\", .{ errors, warnings, infos });\n\n            if (cmd_args.limit) |limit| {\n                if (issues.items.len > limit) {\n                    try ctx.output.print(\"(showing {d} of {d}, use --limit to see more)\\n\", .{ limit, issues.items.len });\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintIdFormats(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (!id_mod.validateId(issue.id)) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"id_format\",\n                .message = \"Invalid issue ID format\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintOrphanedHierarchy(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (orphans.getParentId(issue.id)) |parent_id| {\n            if (!store.id_index.contains(parent_id)) {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"warning\",\n                    .category = \"orphan_hierarchy\",\n                    .message = \"Parent issue does not exist\",\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintOrphanedDependencies(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n            if (!store.id_index.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"warning\",\n                    .category = \"orphan_dependency\",\n                    .message = \"Dependency references non-existent issue\",\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintCircularDependencies(\n    ctx: *CommandContext,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    var graph = ctx.createGraph();\n    const cycles = try graph.detectCycles();\n    defer if (cycles) |c| allocator.free(c);\n\n    if (cycles) |cycle_list| {\n        if (cycle_list.len > 0) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = null,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"circular_dependency\",\n                .message = \"Circular dependencies detected in dependency graph\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintTitles(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (issue.title.len == 0) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"error\",\n                .category = \"empty_title\",\n                .message = \"Issue has empty title\",\n            });\n        } else if (issue.title.len > 500) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"long_title\",\n                .message = \"Title exceeds 500 character limit\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintDuplicateHashes(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    var hash_map = std.StringHashMap([]const u8).init(allocator);\n    defer hash_map.deinit();\n\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        if (issue.content_hash) |hash| {\n            if (hash_map.get(hash)) |existing_id| {\n                try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .severity = \"info\",\n                    .category = \"duplicate_hash\",\n                    .message = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"Duplicate content hash with {s}\", .{existing_id}),\n                });\n            } else {\n                try hash_map.put(hash, issue.id);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintStatusConsistency(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        // Closed issues should have closed_at timestamp\n        if (issue.status.eql(.closed) and issue.closed_at.value == null) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"status_consistency\",\n                .message = \"Closed issue missing closed_at timestamp\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Deferred issues should have defer_until\n        if (issue.status.eql(.deferred) and issue.defer_until.value == null) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"info\",\n                .category = \"status_consistency\",\n                .message = \"Deferred issue missing defer_until date\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn lintTimestamps(\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged(LintIssue),\n) !void {\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    const one_day_future = now + (24 * 60 * 60);\n\n    for (store.issues.items) |issue| {\n        if (issue.status.eql(.tombstone)) continue;\n\n        // Check for timestamps too far in the future (more than 1 day)\n        if (issue.created_at.value > one_day_future) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"future_timestamp\",\n                .message = \"created_at timestamp is in the future\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        if (issue.updated_at.value > one_day_future) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"future_timestamp\",\n                .message = \"updated_at timestamp is in the future\",\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Check that updated_at >= created_at\n        if (issue.updated_at.value < issue.created_at.value) {\n            try issues.append(allocator, .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .severity = \"warning\",\n                .category = \"timestamp_order\",\n                .message = \"updated_at is before created_at\",\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"LintResult struct works\" {\n    const result = LintResult{\n        .success = true,\n        .errors = 0,\n        .warnings = 0,\n        .infos = 0,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(result.success);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), result.errors);\n}\n\ntest \"LintIssue struct works\" {\n    const issue = LintIssue{\n        .id = \"bd-abc\",\n        .severity = \"error\",\n        .category = \"id_format\",\n        .message = \"Invalid ID\",\n    };\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc\", issue.id.?);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"error\", issue.severity);\n}\n\ntest \"run detects uninitialized workspace\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const cmd_args = args.LintArgs{};\n    const global = args.GlobalOptions{ .silent = true, .data_path = \"/nonexistent/path\" };\n\n    const result = run(cmd_args, global, allocator);\n    try std.testing.expectError(LintError.WorkspaceNotInitialized, result);\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":105,"oldLines":7,"newStart":105,"newLines":7,"lines":[" ","             for (display_issues) |issue| {","                 const icon = if (std.mem.eql(u8, displays schema...# beads_zig Storage Schema\n\nStorage Type: JSONL (JSON Lines)\n\n## Files\n\n- `.beads/beads.jsonl` - Main issue storage (git-tracked)\n- `.beads/beads.wal` - Write-ahead log (gitignored)\n- `.beads/beads.lock` - Lock file for flock (gitignored)\n\n## Issue (beads.jsonl)\n\nOne JSON object per line in the main JSONL file.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|-------|------|----------|-------------|\n| id | string | yes | Issue ID (bd-XXXXX format) |\n| content_hash | string | no | SHA256 hash for deduplication |\n| title | string | yes | Issue title (1-500 chars) |\n| description | string | no | Detailed description |\n| design | string | no | Design notes |\n| acceptance_criteria | string | no | Definition of done |\n| notes | string | no | Additional notes |\n| status | string | yes | open, in_progress, blocked, deferred, closed, tombstone, pinned |\n| priority | number | yes | 0 (critical) to 4 (backlog) |\n| issue_type | string | yes | task, bug, feature, epic, chore, docs, question |\n| assignee | string | no | Assigned user |\n| owner | string | no | Issue owner |\n| created_at | string | yes | RFC3339 timestamp |\n| created_by | string | no | Creator |\n| updated_at | string | yes | RFC3339 timestamp |\n| closed_at | string | no | RFC3339 timestamp when closed |\n| close_reason | string | no | Reason for closing |\n| due_at | string | no | RFC3339 due date |\n| defer_until | string | no | RFC3339 defer date |\n| estimated_minutes | number | no | Time estimate |\n| external_ref | string | no | External tracker link |\n| source_system | string | no | Import source |\n| pinned | boolean | yes | High-priority display flag |\n| is_template | boolean | yes | Template flag |\n| labels | array | yes | String array of labels |\n| dependencies | array | yes | Array of Dependency objects |\n| comments | array | yes | Array of Comment objects |\n\n## WAL Entry (beads.wal)\n\nWrite-ahead log for concurrent writes.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Description |\n|-------|------|-------------|\n| op | string | add, update, close, reopen, delete, set_blocked, unset_blocked |\n| ts | number | Unix timestamp for ordering |\n| id | string | Issue ID |\n| data | object | Full Issue object (for add/update) or null |\n\n## Dependency\n\nEmbedded in Issue.dependencies array.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Description |\n|-------|------|-------------|\n| issue_id | string | Dependent issue |\n| depends_on_id | string | Blocker issue |\n| dep_type | string | blocks, parent_child, waits_for, related, etc. |\n| created_at | string | RFC3339 timestamp |\n| created_by | string | Creator |\n| metadata | string | JSON blob for extra data |\n| thread_id | string | Optional thread reference |\n\n## Comment\n\nEmbedded in Issue.comments array.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Description |\n|-------|------|-------------|\n| id | number | Comment ID |\n| issue_id | string | Parent issue ID |\n| author | string | Comment author |\n| body | string | Comment text |\n| created_at | string | RFC3339 timestamp |\nOK\n265/583 cli.schema.test.run with json Add to ~/.bashrc: source <(bz completions bash)\n\n_bz_completions() {\n    local cur prev words cword\n    _init_completion || return\n\n    local commands=\"init create q show update close reopen delete list ready blocked search stale count dep label comments history audit sync config info stats doctor orphans lint version schema completions\"\n\n    if [[ $cword -eq 1 ]]; then\n        COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$commands\" -- \"$cur\"))\n        return\n    fi\n\n    case ${words[1]} in\n        show|update|close|reopen|delete|comments|history)\n            # Complete with issue IDs\n            local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        dep)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list tree cycles\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        label)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list list-all\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        comments)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add list\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        config)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"get set list\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        sync)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--flush-only --import-only\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        completions)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"bash zsh fish powershell\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        create)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--priority --type --assignee --label --dep\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        list)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--status --priority --type --assignee --label --all --limit --offset\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        stale)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--days\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        count)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--by\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n    esac\n}\n\ncomplete -F _bz_completions bz\nOK\n271/583 cli.completions.test.run generates zsh completions...#compdef bz\n# zsh completion for bz (beads_zig)\n# Add to ~/.zshrc: source <(bz completions zsh)\n\n_bz() {\n    local -a commands\n    commands=(\n        'init:Initialize beads workspace'\n        'create:Create new issue'\n        'q:Quick capture (create + print ID only)'\n        'show:Display issue details'\n        'update:Update issue fields'\n        'close:Close an issue'\n        'reopen:Reopen a closed issue'\n        'delete:Soft delete (tombstone)'\n        'list:List issues with filters'\n        'ready:Show actionable issues (unblocked)'\n        'blocked:Show blocked issues'\n        'search:Full-text search'\n        'stale:Find stale issues'\n        'count:Count issues'\n        'dep:Manage dependencies'\n        'label:Manage labels'\n        'comments:Manage comments'\n        'history:Show issue history'\n        'audit:View audit log'\n        'sync:Sync with JSONL file'\n        'config:Manage configuration'\n        'info:Workspace info'\n        'stats:Project statistics'\n        'doctor:Run diagnostics'\n        'orphans:Find orphaned issues'\n        'lint:Validate database consistency'\n        'version:Show version'\n        'schema:View storage schema'\n        'completions:Generate shell completions'\n    )\n\n    local -a global_opts\n    global_opts=(\n        '--json[Output in JSON format]'\n        '--toon[Output in TOON format]'\n        '-q[Quiet mode]'\n        '--quiet[Quiet mode]'\n        '-v[Verbose mode]'\n        '--verbose[Verbose mode]'\n        '--no-color[Disable colors]'\n        '--data[Override .beads/ directory]:directory:_files -/'\n    )\n\n    _arguments -C \\\n        $global_opts \\\n        '1:command:->command' \\\n        '*::arg:->args'\n\n    case $state in\n        command)\n            _describe 'command' commands\n            ;;\n        args)\n            case ${words[1]} in\n                show|update|close|reopen|delete)\n                    _arguments '1:issue ID:($(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null))'\n                    ;;\n                dep)\n                    local -a dep_cmds\n                    dep_cmds=('add:Add dependency' 'remove:Remove dependency' 'list:List dependencies' 'tree:Show dependency tree' 'cycles:Detect cycles')\n                    _describe 'subcommand' dep_cmds\n                    ;;\n                label)\n                    local -a label_cmds\n                    label_cmds=('add:Add labels' 'remove:Remove labels' 'list:List labels' 'list-all:List all labels')\n                    _describe 'subcommand' label_cmds\n                    ;;\n                completions)\n                    local -a shells\n                    shells=('bash' 'zsh' 'fish' 'powershell')\n                    _describe 'shell' shells\n                    ;;\n            esac\n            ;;\n    esac\n}\n\n_bz\nOK\n272/583 displays schema...# beads_zig Storage Schema\n\nStorage Type: JSONL (JSON Lines)\n\n## Files\n\n- `.beads/beads.jsonl` - Main issue storage (git-tracked)\n- `.beads/beads.wal` - Write-ahead log (gitignored)\n- `.beads/beads.lock` - Lock file for flock (gitignored)\n\n## Issue (beads.jsonl)\n\nOne JSON object per line in the main JSONL file.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|-------|------|----------|-------------|\n| id | string | yes | Issue ID (bd-XXXXX format) |\n| content_hash | string | no | SHA256 hash for deduplication |\n| title | string | yes | Issue title (1-500 chars) |\n| description | string | no | Detailed description |\n| design | string | no | Design notes |\n| acceptance_criteria | string | no | Definition of done |\n| notes | string | no | Additional notes |\n| status | string | yes | open, in_progress, blocked, deferred, closed, tombstone, pinned |\n| priority | number | yes | 0 (critical) to 4 (backlog) |\n| issue_type | string | yes | task, bug, feature, epic, chore, docs, question |\n| assignee | string | no | Assigned user |\n| owner | string | no | Issue owner |\n| created_at | string | yes | RFC3339 timestamp |\n| created_by | string | no | Creator |\n| updated_at | string | yes | RFC3339 timestamp |\n| closed_at | string | no | RFC3339 timestamp when closed |\n| close_reason | string | no | Reason for closing |\n| due_at | string | no | RFC3339 due date |\n| defer_until | string | no | RFC3339 defer date |\n| estimated_minutes | number | no | Time estimate |\n| external_ref | string | no | External tracker delete list ready blocked search stale count dep label comments history audit sync config info stats doctor orphans lint version schema completions\"\n\n    if [[ $cword -eq 1 ]]; then\n      'show:Display issue details'\n        'update:Update issue fields'\n        'close:Close an issue'\n        'reopen:Reopen a closed issue'\n        'delete:Soft delete (tombstone)'\n local -a global_opts\n    global_opts=(\n        '--json[Output in JSON format]'\n        '--toon[Output in TOON format]'\n        '-q[Quiet mode]'\n        '--quiet[Quiet mode]'\n        '-v[Verbose Description |\n|-------|------|----------|-------------|\n| id | string | yes | Issue ID (bd-XXXXX format) |\n| content_hash | string | no | SHA256 hash for deduplication |\n| title | string | yes | Add to ~/.bashrc: source <(bz completions bash)\n\n_bz_completions() {\n    local cur prev words cword\n    _init_completion || return\n\n    local commands=\"init create q show update close reopen delete list ready blocked search stale count dep label comments history audit sync config info stats doctor orphans lint version schema completions\"\n\n    if [[ $cword -eq 1 ]]; then\n        COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$commands\" -- \"$cur\"))\n        return\n    fi\n\n    case ${words[1]} in\n        show|update|close|reopen|delete|comments|history)\n            # Complete with issue IDs\n            local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        dep)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list tree cycles\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        label)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list list-all\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        comments)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add list\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        config)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"get set list\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        sync)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--flush-only --import-only\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        completions)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"bash zsh fish powershell\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        create)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--priority --type --assignee --label --dep\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        list)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--status --priority --type --assignee --label --all --limit --offset\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        stale)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--days\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        count)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--by\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n    esac\n}\n\ncomplete -F _bz_completions bz\nOK\n271/583 cli.completions.test.run generates zsh completions...#compdef bz\n# zsh completion for bz (beads_zig)\n# Add to ~/.zshrc: source <(bz completions zsh)\n\n_bz() {\n    local -a commands\n    commands=(\n        'init:Initialize beads workspace'\n        'create:Create new issue'\n        'q:Quick capture (create + print ID only)'\n        'show:Display issue details'\n        'update:Update issue fields'\n        'close:Close an issue'\n        'reopen:Reopen a closed issue'\n        'delete:Soft delete (tombstone)'\n
